Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown remarkable performance in various robotic tasks, as they can perceive visual information and understand natural language instructions. However, when applied to robotics, VLMs remain subject to a fundamental limitation inherent in large language models (LLMs): they struggle with numerical reasoning, particularly in object detection and object-state localization. To explore numerical reasoning as a regression task in VLMs, we propose a novel training strategy to adapt VLMs for object detection and object-state localization. This approach leverages box decoder outputs to compute an Auxiliary Regression Loss (ARL) during fine-tuning, while preserving standard sequence prediction at inference. We leverage this training strategy to develop StateVLM (State-aware Vision-Language Model), a novel model designed to perceive and learn fine-grained object representations, including precise localization of objects and their states, as well as graspable regions. Due to the lack of a benchmark for object-state affordance reasoning, we introduce an open-source benchmark, Object State Affordance Reasoning (OSAR), which contains 1,172 scenes with 7,746 individual objects and corresponding bounding boxes. Comparative experiments on adapted benchmarks (RefCOCO, RefCOCO+, and \mbox{RefCOCOg}) demonstrate that ARL improves model performance by an average of 1.6\% compared to models without ARL. Experiments on the OSAR benchmark further support this finding, showing that StateVLM with ARL achieves an average of 5.2\% higher performance than models without ARL. In particular, ARL is also important for the complex task of affordance reasoning in OSAR, where it enhances the consistency of model outputs.

Abstract: We propose HeadsUp, a scalable feed-forward method for reconstructing high-quality 3D Gaussian heads from large-scale multi-camera setups. This latent representation is then decoded into a set of UV-parameterized 3D Gaussians anchored to a neutral head template. This UV representation decouples the number of 3D Gaussians from the number and resolution of input images, enabling training with many high-resolution input views. We train and evaluate our model on an internal dataset with more than 10,000 subjects, which is an order of magnitude larger than existing multi-view human head datasets. HeadsUp achieves state-of-the-art reconstruction quality and generalizes to novel identities without test-time optimization. We extensively analyze the scaling behavior of our model across identities, views, and model capacity, revealing practical insights for quality-compute trade-offs. ### [57] [Large Language Models are Universal Reasoners for Visual Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04040)
*Sucheng Ren,Chen Chen,Zhenbang Wang,Liangchen Song,Xiangxin Zhu,Alan Yuille,Liang-Chieh Chen,Jiasen Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出UniReasoner框架，利用LLM作为通用推理器弥合文本到图像生成中的理解-生成差距：LLM先生成视觉草稿，然后进行自我批评生成文本评估，最后扩散模型联合条件于文本、草稿和评估进行生成，有效提升了组合对齐和语义忠实度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到图像生成系统尽管在架构上实现了统一（LLM同时处理视觉理解和生成），但存在理解-生成差距：模型能准确判断图像是否满足复杂提示，却无法在生成时忠实对齐这些提示。作者旨在利用LLM自身的理解优势来指导生成过程。

Method: UniReasoner包含三个步骤：(1) LLM先生成离散视觉token构成的粗粒度视觉草稿；(2) LLM对草稿进行自我批评，评估其与提示的一致性，生成定位具体问题的文本评估；(3) 扩散模型联合条件于原始提示、视觉草稿和文本评估进行生成。草稿缓解了纯文本条件中的欠指定问题，评估则将验证转化为可操作的正确性信号。

Result: 在相同扩散主干下，UniReasoner显著提升了组合对齐和语义忠实度，同时保持了图像质量，有效缩小了理解-生成差距。

Conclusion: 利用LLM推理能力弥合理解与生成之间的差距是可行且有效的，为文本到图像生成中利用语言模型推理提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Text-to-image generation has advanced rapidly with diffusion models, progressing from CLIP and T5 conditioning to unified systems where a single LLM backbone handles both visual understanding and generation. Despite the architectural unification, these systems frequently fail to faithfully align complex prompts during synthesis, even though they remain highly accurate at verifying whether an image satisfies those same prompts. We formalize this as the \emph{understanding-generation gap} and propose UniReasoner, a framework that leverages the LLM as a universal reasoner to convert its understanding strength into direct generation guidance. Given a prompt, the LLM first produces a coarse visual draft composed of discrete vision tokens. It then performs a self-critique by evaluating the draft for prompt consistency, producing a grounded textual evaluation that pinpoints what needs to be corrected. Finally, a diffusion model is conditioned jointly on the prompt, the visual draft, and the evaluation, ensuring that generation is guided by explicit corrective signals. Each signal addresses a limitation of the other: the draft provides a concrete, scene-level anchor that reduces under-specification in text-only conditioning, while the evaluation turns verification into grounded, actionable constraints that correct omissions, hallucinations, and relational errors. Experiments show that UniReasoner improves compositional alignment and semantic faithfulness under the same diffusion backbone while maintaining image quality, demonstrating a practical way to exploit LLM reasoning to close the understanding-generation gap.

Motivation: 音视频智能（AVI）作为人工智能的前沿领域，在大型基础模型时代愈发重要，但文献碎片化严重，任务分类不一致、评估标准不统一，阻碍了系统比较与知识整合，亟需一份全面的综述来建立统一框架。

Method: 采用文献综述方法，通过建立统一的AVI任务分类体系（理解、生成、交互三大类），系统梳理方法论基础（模态分词、跨模态融合、自回归/扩散生成、大规模预训练、指令对齐、偏好优化），并整理数据集、基准和评估指标，进行结构化比较。

Result: 建立了统一的AVI任务分类体系，涵盖理解（语音识别、声音定位等）、生成（音频驱动视频合成、视频转音频等）和交互（对话、具身/智能体接口）三大任务族；系统总结了核心方法论；整理了代表性数据集、基准和评估指标；识别了同步性、空间推理、可控性和安全性等开放挑战。

Conclusion: 本文通过整合碎片化的AVI研究领域，提供了一个连贯的框架性参考，为该领域的未来研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Audio-Visual Intelligence (AVI) has emerged as a central frontier in artificial intelligence, bridging auditory and visual modalities to enable machines that can perceive, generate, and interact in the multimodal real world. In the era of large foundation models, joint modeling of audio and vision has become increasingly crucial, i.e., not only for understanding but also for controllable generation and reasoning across dynamic, temporally grounded signals. Recent advances, such as Meta MovieGen and Google Veo-3, highlight the growing industrial and academic focus on unified audio-vision architectures that learn from massive multimodal data. However, despite rapid progress, the literature remains fragmented, spanning diverse tasks, inconsistent taxonomies, and heterogeneous evaluation practices that impede systematic comparison and knowledge integration. This survey provides the first comprehensive review of AVI through the lens of large foundation models. We establish a unified taxonomy covering the broad landscape of AVI tasks, ranging from understanding (e.g., speech recognition, sound localization) to generation (e.g., audio-driven video synthesis, video-to-audio) and interaction (e.g., dialogue, embodied, or agentic interfaces). We synthesize methodological foundations, including modality tokenization, cross-modal fusion, autoregressive and diffusion-based generation, large-scale pretraining, instruction alignment, and preference optimization. Furthermore, we curate representative datasets, benchmarks, and evaluation metrics, offering a structured comparison across task families and identifying open challenges in synchronization, spatial reasoning, controllability, and safety. By consolidating this rapidly expanding field into a coherent framework, this survey aims to serve as a foundational reference for future research on large-scale AVI.

</details>

### [59] [When Should a Language Model Trust Itself? Same-Model Self-Verification as a Conditional Confidence Signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02915)
*Aditya Ajay Phalod*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了同模型自我验证（self-verification）作为选择性预测置信度信号的有效性，将其与LL-AVG和LL-SUM两个强似然基线在ARC-Challenge和TruthfulQA-MC数据集上进行比较。结果发现自我验证的效果高度依赖任务类型、模型家族、规模及提示形式，并非通用不确定性估计器，而是一种条件性置信信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同模型自我验证作为一种置信度信号，在选择性预测中的实际价值尚不明确，尤其当考虑强似然基线时，需要系统评估其有效性和局限性。

Method: 在ARC-Challenge和TruthfulQA-MC数据集上，对多个模型家族、规模和提示变体，将自我验证与LL-AVG和LL-SUM两个基线进行对比评估。使用正确性排序以及AURC和操作点分析来测量弃权质量。

Result: 在ARC-Challenge上，自我验证对Phi-2和Qwen模型显著优于LL-AVG，Qwen-7B提升最大。在TruthfulQA-MC上，信号可靠性较差：小模型对提示敏感，DeepSeek-R1-Distill-8B相比LL-AVG退化，LL-SUM通常是更强的基线。

Conclusion: 自我验证不应被视为通用不确定性估计器，而是一种条件性置信信号，其价值取决于任务类型、模型家族、提示形式以及需要超越的基线。

Abstract: Same-model self-verification, prompting a model to audit its own predicted answer, is a plausible confidence signal for selective prediction, but its practical value remains unclear once strong likelihood-based baselines are taken seriously. We evaluate self-verification against two such baselines, LL-AVG and LL-SUM, on ARC-Challenge and TruthfulQA-MC across multiple model families, scales, and prompt variants. We measure not only correctness ranking, but also abstention quality through AURC and operating-point analyses. The results are sharply task- and model-dependent. On ARC-Challenge, self-verification substantially improves over LL-AVG for Phi-2 and the Qwen models, with the largest gains appearing in Qwen-7B. On TruthfulQA-MC, however, the signal is less reliable: smaller models can become prompt-sensitive, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-8B degrades relative to LL-AVG, and LL-SUM often remains the stronger practical baseline. We therefore do not treat self-verification as a general-purpose uncertainty estimator. In this setting, it is better understood as a conditional confidence signal whose value depends on task type, model family, prompt formulation, and, crucially, the baseline it must beat.

</details>


### [60] [Evaluating Reasoning Models for Queries with Presuppositions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03050)
*Rose Sathyanathan,Kinshuk Vasisht,Danish Pruthi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型推理模型（LRMs）在面对包含事实错误预设的用户查询时，能否识别并质疑这些错误假设。通过构建涵盖健康、科学和通用知识的预设查询数据集进行测试，发现推理模型比非推理模型准确率略高（2-11%），但仍无法质疑26-42%的错误预设，且受预设表达强度影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大量用户查询包含事实不准确的假设，而先前的LLM往往无法质疑这些错误假设，可能强化用户的错误认知。随着推理模型能力提升，作者重新审视这类模型能否推理出潜在假设并恰当回应用户。

Method: 构建包含不同程度预设（健康、科学、通用知识）的查询数据集，在多个广泛部署的模型上进行评估，比较推理模型与非推理模型的表现。

Result: 推理模型准确率比非推理模型高2-11%，但仍无法质疑26-42%的错误预设；模型表现受预设表达强度影响。

Conclusion: 尽管推理模型在识别错误预设方面有所改进，但仍有很大比例的虚假预设未被质疑，且对预设表达强度敏感，说明该问题尚未得到充分解决。

Abstract: Millions of users turn to AI models for their information needs. It is conceivable that a large number of user queries contain assumptions that may be factually inaccurate. Prior work notes that large language models (LLMs) often fail to challenge such erroneous assumptions, and can reinforce users' misinformed opinions. However, given the recent advances, especially in model's reasoning capabilities, we revisit whether large reasoning models (LRMs) can reason about the underlying assumptions and respond to user queries appropriately. We construct queries with varying degrees of presuppositions spanning health, science, and general knowledge, and use it to evaluate several widely-deployed models When compared to non-reasoning models, we find that reasoning models achieve a slightly higher accuracy (2-11%), but they still fail to challenge a large fraction (26-42%) of false presuppositions. Further, reasoning models remain susceptible to how strongly the presupposition is expressed.

</details>


### [61] [How Language Models Process Negation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03052)
*Zhejian Zhou,Tianyi Zhou,Robin Jia,Jonathan May*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了LLM处理否定的机制，发现模型内部存在正确处理否定的组件，但后期注意力层偏好简单捷径导致准确率低；通过消融这些注意力模块可显著提升否定相关问题的准确率。模型同时采用两种机制：抑制机制（关注被否定短语并抑制相关概念）和构建机制（直接构建否定短语的整体表征），其中构建机制占主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM在处理否定（negation）时的内部工作机制，包括模型为何在否定问题上准确率低，以及模型内部如何表征和处理否定语义。

Method: 在Mistral-7B和Llama-3.1-8B上，综合运用观察性和因果性可解释性技术，包括注意力模块消融实验，以及两种机制假设（抑制机制 vs 构建机制）的对比分析。

Result: 1）模型内部存在正确处理否定的组件，但后期注意力层倾向于简单捷径导致错误答案，消融这些模块可提升准确率；2）模型同时使用抑制机制和构建机制处理否定，其中构建机制更为显著。

Conclusion: LLM处理否定时存在多种竞争机制共存的现象，构建式（constructive）计算占主导地位，深化了对LLM内部否定处理机制的理解。

Abstract: We study how Large Language Models (LLMs) process negation mechanistically. First, we establish that even though open-weight models often provide wrong answers to questions involving negation, they do possess internal components that process negation correctly. Their poor accuracy is due to late-layer attention behavior that promotes simple shortcuts; ablating those attention modules greatly improves accuracy on negation-related questions. Second, we uncover how models process negation. We consider two hypotheses: models could use attention heads that attend to the phrase being negated and suppress related concepts, or they could directly construct a representation of the entire negative phrase (e.g., representing "not gas" as a vector that promotes liquids and solids). We apply a range of observational and causal interpretability techniques on Mistral-7B and Llama-3.1-8B to show that models implement both mechanisms, with the "constructive" mechanism being more prominent. Combined, our work deepens the understanding of LLMs' internals, highlighting construction-dominant computations and the coexistence of competing mechanisms within LLMs.

</details>


### [62] [The TTS-STT Flywheel: Synthetic Entity-Dense Audio Closes the Indic ASR Gap Where Commercial and Open-Source Systems Fail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03073)
*Venkata Pushpak Teja Menta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对小领域印地语ASR（数字串、货币金额、地址、品牌名、英印混合语）表现不佳的问题，本文提出自包含TTS→STT飞轮：以<50美元成本合成~22,000条实体密集的英印混合语音，对vasista22/whisper-telugu-large-v2进行LoRA微调，在Telugu测试集上实体命中率从0.027提升至0.473（17倍于开源SOTA，3倍于商业系统），读散文WER退化控制在+6.6 pp以内。跨语言测试也展现显著提升，但均未达到预设目标。通过消融实验验证了~100%增益来自合成语料。同时发现Vanilla Whisper-large-v3存在Telugu特定脚本坍塌问题，可由逐语言LoRA修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小领域（niche-domain）的印地语ASR任务，包括数字串、货币金额、地址、品牌名以及英语/印地语代码混合（code-mix）场景，无论是开源SOTA还是商业系统都表现不佳。例如Telugu测试集上开源SOTA（vasista22/whisper-telugu-large-v2）的实体命中率仅0.027，商业系统Deepgram Nova-3也仅0.16，存在巨大差距需要弥合。

Method: 提出一个自包含的TTS→STT飞轮（flywheel）：（1）使用开源Indic TTS管线合成约22,000条实体密集的英印代码混合话语，边际成本低于50美元；（2）在vasista22/whisper-telugu-large-v2基础上进行LoRA微调。同时进行了消融实验（仅在FLEURS-Te上LoRA训练）和native人类录制验证（n=20 Telugu）。

Result: Telugu测试集：EHR从0.027（开源SOTA）和0.16（商业）提升至0.473，分别提升17倍和3倍；读散文WER退化控制在+6.6 pp以内。跨语言：beta-Hi EHR 0.337（7倍于vasista22），beta-Ta EHR 0.543（22倍于vasista22，22倍于Deepgram）。但所有三个beta模型均未达到预注册的EHR目标（Te 0.75, Hi/Ta 0.65）。Native人类录制验证：beta-Te EHR 0.516（vs synth 0.473）。消融实验：仅有FLEURS-Te的LoRA训练仅获得EHR 0.020，约100%增益归因于EDSA语料。此外发现Vanilla Whisper-large-v3在Telugu上存在脚本坍塌（SFR 0.46-0.71），可由逐语言LoRA修正（SFR 0.81-0.97），但在印地语和泰米尔语上不适用。

Conclusion: 所提出的自包含TTS→STT飞轮能够以极低成本显著提升小领域印地语ASR的实体识别能力，在Telugu和Tamil上大幅超越开源SOTA和商业系统，但在Hindi上因商业系统已有充分实体覆盖而表现不足。所有模型均未达到预设目标，需进一步改进。研究还揭示了Whisper模型在Telugu上的脚本坍塌问题及其修正方案。代码、测试集、预测结果、EDSA语料和实体词典均开源发布。

Abstract: Niche-domain Indic ASR -- digit strings, currency amounts, addresses, brand names, English/Indic codemix -- is under-served by both open-source SOTA and commercial systems. On a synthesised entity-dense Telugu test set (held-out by synthesis system), vasista22/whisper-telugu-large-v2 (open SOTA) achieves Entity-Hit-Rate (EHR) 0.027 and Deepgram Nova-3 (commercial) 0.16. We close this gap with a self-contained TTS<->STT flywheel: an open-source Indic TTS pipeline synthesises ~22,000 entity-dense Indic-English code-mix utterances at <$50 marginal cost, and a LoRA fine-tune on top of vasista22 achieves EHR 0.473 on the held-out test (17x over open SOTA, 3x over commercial), with read-prose regression bounded to +6.6 pp WER on FLEURS-Te. Cross-language: beta-Hi 0.337 (7x vs vasista22) and beta-Ta 0.543 (22x vs vasista22, 22x vs Deepgram); on Hindi where Deepgram has substantial entity coverage, the flywheel underperforms commercial. All three beta models fall below pre-registered EHR targets (0.75 for Te, 0.65 for Hi/Ta); we report honestly. A native-human-recorded sanity check (n=20 Telugu) confirms transfer to real speech (beta-Te EHR 0.516 on native vs 0.473 on synth). An EDSA-isolation ablation (LoRA on FLEURS-Te alone) yields EHR 0.020 on the same held-out, attributing ~100% of the gain to the EDSA corpus. We additionally report a language-conditional finding: vanilla Whisper-large-v3 has Telugu-specific Script Collapse (SFR 0.46-0.71) that a per-language LoRA corrects (SFR 0.81-0.97), but the recipe is contraindicated on Hindi and Tamil where vanilla SFR >= 0.98. Code, holdouts, predictions, EDSA corpus, and entity dictionaries are released open-source.

</details>


### [63] [MedStruct-S: A Benchmark for Key Discovery, Key-Conditioned QA and Semi-Structured Extraction from OCR Clinical Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03103)
*Yingyun Li,Yu Wang,Haiyang Qian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了MedStruct-S基准，用于评估OCR临床报告中半结构化信息提取的三个任务（字段标题发现、基于键的条件问答、端到端键值对提取），涵盖未知键和OCR噪声场景。对四种仅编码器模型和五种仅解码器模型（0.11B-103B参数）的基准测试表明：仅编码器模型在非空值键条件问答中表现最佳且参数更小；同量级下仅编码器模型整体更优；未控制模型规模时，微调的仅解码器模型总体最强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法未能充分考虑两个关键因素：异构且不完全已知的键表示，以及OCR引入的噪声，导致难以评估模型在真实场景中的鲁棒性。

Method: 构建包含3,582张标注真实临床报告页面的MedStruct-S基准，在未知键和OCR噪声条件下评估三个子任务；对比仅编码器序列标注+后处理与仅解码器结构化生成两种范式，涵盖4种编码器模型和5种解码器模型。

Result: 仅编码器模型在非空值键条件问答任务上表现最佳且参数规模远小于仅解码器模型；同量级对比中仅编码器模型整体更优；不控制模型规模时，微调后的仅解码器模型获得最强总体结果。

Conclusion: MedStruct-S为半结构化IE场景下的模型选择和比较提供了可靠且实用的基准。

Abstract: Semi-structured information extraction (IE) from OCR-derived clinical reports is crucial for efficiently reconstructing patients' longitudinal medical histories. In practice, this scenario commonly involves three tasks: (i) field-header (key) discovery, (ii) key-conditioned question answering (QA), and (iii) end-to-end key-value pair extraction. However, existing evaluations often under-model two factors: heterogeneous and incompletely known key representations, and OCR-induced noise. This makes it difficult to assess model robustness in real-world settings.
  We present MedStruct-S, a benchmark specifically designed to evaluate these tasks under unknown keys and OCR noise. MedStruct-S contains 3,582 annotated real-world clinical report pages. Using MedStruct-S, we benchmark two representative paradigms: encoder-only sequence labeling with post-processing and decoder-only structured generation, covering four encoder-only and five decoder-only models spanning 0.11B to 103B parameters. Our results show that encoder-only models achieve the best performance for non-null-value key-conditioned QA despite being substantially smaller than decoder-only models. When comparing models of similar order of magnitude, encoder-only models still perform better overall. Without controlling for model scale, fine-tuned decoder-only models deliver the strongest overall results. These findings show that the benchmark provides a reliable and practical basis for selecting and comparing models across different semi-structured IE settings.

</details>


### [64] [Effective Performance Measurement: Challenges and Opportunities in KPI Extraction from Earnings Calls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03147)
*Rasmus T. Aavang,Rasmus Tjalk-Bøggild,Alexandre Iolov,Giovanni Rizzi,Mike Zhang,Johannes Bjerva*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 财报电话会议是上市公司财务信息的重要来源，但其非结构化、无标签且使用会话语言的特点使得信息提取极具挑战性，不同于SEC要求的模板化 filings。

Method: 1) 评估SEC训练模型在SEC数据集上的泛化能力；2) 引入三个新基准：SECB、ECB和包含2460个专家标注组的ECB-A；3) 提出基于LLM的系统进行开放式信息提取，并通过人工评估验证。

Abstract: Earnings calls are a key source of financial information about public companies. However, extracting information from these calls is difficult. Unlike the templatic filings required by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (SEC) to report a company's financial situation, earnings conference calls have no built-in labels, are unstructured, and feature conversational language. We explore this challenging domain by assessing the information captured by models trained on SEC filings and in-context learning methods. To establish a baseline, we first evaluate the generalization capabilities of SEC-trained models across established SEC datasets. To support our investigation, we introduce three novel benchmarks: (1) SEC Filings Benchmark (SECB), (2) Earnings Calls Benchmark (ECB), and ECB-A, a subset with 2,460 expert annotation groups to support our qualitative analysis. We find that encoder-based models struggle with the domain shift. ### [65] [Geometric Deviation as an Unsupervised Pre-Generation Reliability Signal: Probing LLM Representations for Answerability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03196)
*Yucheng Du*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究能否通过表示几何（隐藏状态偏离可回答参考集的程度）作为预生成信号来判断查询是否超出模型知识范围。实验发现该信号在数学类提示中表现良好（ROC-AUC 0.78-0.84），在事实类提示中无效，编码类提示中效果显著但方差较大。信号主要出现在早期层并逐渐衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的语言模型应在生成前就能判断查询是否超出其知识范围。现有方法通常需要标注失败数据或访问模型输出，作者希望利用表示几何这一轻量级、无需额外数据的预生成信号来解决这一问题。

Method: 通过测量隐藏状态与可回答参考集（answerable reference set）质心之间的几何偏差，作为预生成信号。在三个指令微调模型（Llama 3.1-8B, Qwen 2.5-7B, Mistral-7B-Instruct）和三种提示形式（数学、事实、代码）上进行实验，进行逐层分析。

Result: 数学提示下几何偏差信号表现稳定（ROC-AUC 0.78-0.84），优于简单拒绝基线，与self-consistency相当；事实提示下无可靠信号；代码提示下效果显著但方差较大。信号在早期层出现并向输出层逐渐衰减。

Conclusion: 几何偏差可作为轻量级预生成信号，在具有形式化可回答性约束的结构化领域（如数学）中可靠，但在事实类查询中不适用，存在明确的泛化边界。

Abstract: A reliable language model should be able to signal, prior to generation, when a query falls outside its knowledge. We investigate whether representation geometry can provide such a pre-generation signal by measuring the deviation of hidden states from an answerable reference set, requiring no labeled failure data and no access to model outputs.
  Across three instruction-tuned models (Llama 3.1-8B, Qwen 2.5-7B, and Mistral-7B-Instruct) and three prompt forms (Math, Fact, Code), we find that geometry primarily encodes task form. Within mathematical prompts, unanswerable inputs consistently deviate from the answerable centroid, yielding strong separation (ROC-AUC 0.78-0.84). This single-pass pre-generation signal outperforms a simple refusal baseline and compares favorably to self-consistency. It also captures cases where models do not explicitly refuse.
  In contrast, no reliable geometric signal emerges for factual prompts, indicating that the effect is form-conditional rather than universal. Code prompts show large effect sizes with higher variance, suggesting partial generalization beyond mathematical form.
  A layer-wise analysis reveals that the signal arises in early layers and gradually attenuates toward the output. These results suggest that answerability-related geometry is established before the final stages of generation. Together, these findings indicate that geometric deviation can serve as a lightweight pre-generation signal that is reliable in structured domains with formal answerability constraints, with clear boundaries on where it generalizes.

</details>

### [71] [An ERP Study of Recursive Possessive Parsing in ASD Children and Its Cognitive Neuro Mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03447)

This ERP study investigated the online processing of two-level recursive possessive structures in Mandarin-speaking children with ASD (n = 12) compared to typically developing (TD) peers (n = 12) using a sentence-picture matching paradigm. ERPs were analyzed for P200 (150-250 ms), N400 (300-500 ms), and P600 (500-1000 ms). Results showed that ASD children exhibited significantly reduced P200 amplitudes and failed to show the typical posterior grammaticality effect, indicating atypical early perceptual processing. No robust N400 violation effect was observed in either group, confirming the mismatch was not a semantic anomaly; however, ASD children showed a reversed anterior effect and an attenuated posterior effect. ### [73] [Detecting Stealth Sycophancy in Mental-Health Dialogue with Dynamic Emotional Signature Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03472)
*Tianze Han,Beining Xu,Hanbo Zhang,Yongming Lu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Dynamic Emotional Signature Graphs (DESG)，一种模型无关的评估器。该方法将对话窗口解耦为临床状态表示，并利用非对称临床几何进行评分。DESG不依赖大语言模型作为最终评判者，而是构建临床状态流形来区分有害、有益和中性响应。

We use a direct LLM judge as a baseline that reads raw dialogue text and predicts whether the target response is harmful, productive, or neutral. We find that direct LLM judges and symmetric text-similarity metrics are poorly aligned with therapeutic quality because the target label depends on clinical direction: whether the response moves the user state toward regulation or reframing, leaves it broadly unchanged, or reinforces deterioration through higher risk affect or cognitive-distortion mass. To address this issue, we propose Dynamic Emotional Signature Graphs (DESG), a model-agnostic evaluator that represents dialogue windows with decoupled clinical states and scores them using asymmetric clinical geometry. We evaluate DESG on a constructed diagnostic stress-test benchmark of 3{,}000 dialogue windows from EmpatheticDialogues, ESConv, and CRADLE-Dialogue, covering peer support, counseling dialogue, and crisis-oriented interaction. On the 600-window held-out test aggregate, DESG-Ensemble achieves 0.9353 macro-F1, exceeding ConcatANN by 1.51 percentage points, BERTScore by 19.63 points, and TRACT by 33.81 points. Feature ablations, artifact controls, a 100-window blinded adjudicator audit, and qualitative disagreement cases indicate that the clinical state manifold is the main discriminative substrate, while graph-based trajectory components provide asymmetric scoring and interpretable diagnostics rather than serving as the sole source of performance.

### [74] [CuraView: A Multi-Agent Framework for Medical Hallucination Detection with GraphRAG-Enhanced Knowledge Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03476)
*Severin Ye,Xiao Kong,Xiaopeng He,Guangsu Yan,Dongsuk Oh*

Motivation: 出院小结需要从冗长的电子健康记录中提取关键信息，手动提取劳动强度大。大语言模型虽能提高生成效率，但易产生与源记录矛盾的"可信度幻觉"，直接危及患者安全。现有方法缺乏细粒度的句子级检测和可解释的证据链。

Method: 提出CuraView多智能体框架：1）从患者级EHR构建基于GraphRAG的知识图谱；2）实现闭环生成-检测流水线，包含句子级证据检索和四等级分类（E1强支持到E4直接矛盾），生成结构化可解释的证据链。

Result: 在Discharge-Me基准的50例测试患者上，微调Qwen3-14B在E4指标上F1=0.831（召回率90.9%，精确率76.5%），E3+E4上F1=0.823，较基模型相对提升50.0%，优于RAGTruth-style和QAGS-style基线。

Conclusion: 基于证据链的图检索验证显著提升了临床文档的事实可靠性，同时可生成可复用的标注数据集，用于下游模型训练和蒸馏。

Abstract: Discharge summaries require extracting critical information from lengthy electronic health records (EHRs), a process that is labor-intensive when performed manually. Large language models (LLMs) can improve generation efficiency; however, they are prone to producing faithfulness hallucinations, statements that contradict source records, posing direct risks to patient safety. To address this, we present CuraView, a multi-agent framework for sentence-level detection and evidence-grounded explanation of faithfulness hallucinations in discharge summaries. CuraView constructs a GraphRAG-based knowledge graph from patient-level EHRs and implements a closed-loop generation-detection pipeline with sentence-level evidence retrieval and classification spanning four evidence grades from strong support to direct contradiction (E1-E4), yielding structured and interpretable evidence chains.
  We evaluate CuraView on a subset of 250 patients from the Discharge-Me benchmark, with 50 patients held out for testing. Our fine-tuned Qwen3-14B detection model achieves an F1 of 0.831 on the safety-critical E4 metric (90.9% recall, 76.5% precision) and an F1 of 0.823 on E3+E4, representing a 50.0% relative improvement over the base model and outperforming RAGTruth-style and QAGS-style baselines. These results demonstrate that evidence-chain-based graph retrieval verification substantially improves the factual reliability of clinical documentation, while simultaneously producing reusable annotated datasets for downstream model training and distillation.

</details>


### [75] [Rational Communication Shapes Morphological Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03510)
*Fengyuan Yang,Yongqian Peng,Yuxi Ma,Chenheng Xu,Yixin Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文在理性言语行为（RSA）框架下，基于COHA和COCA语料库中1820-2019年间4323个英语复合词和派生词，证明词汇化过程中，实际出现的形态组合系统地优于同期可用的替代组合，体现了说话者生产成本与听者可恢复性之间的交际权衡，将理性沟通解释从话语层面扩展至词汇内部结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管交际效率塑造词汇系统已有共识（Gibson et al., 2019），但形态组合（复合/派生）作为历史情境下说话者在竞争性语素序列中的选择，为何语言最终选定某一种语素组合而非其他合理替代，这一问题尚未被建模解释。

Method: 在RSA框架内，使用COHA和COCA构建时间索引词典，生成同期可用的替代形态组合；通过比较实际出现的4323个英语复合词和派生词（1820-2019）与替代组合的排序表现，衡量语义信息性与生产成本整合模型的预测能力。

Result: 整合语义信息性与生产成本的模型在MRR和Acc@k指标上优于纯语义或纯成本基线；语用说话者模型（S₁）相对于纯语义基线的优势随着候选集扩大而增长，表明仅靠语义无法充分确定形态选择。

Conclusion: 词汇化反映了表达性与效率之间的交际权衡，将理性沟通的解释从话语层面选择扩展到了词汇内部结构层面。

Abstract: Human languages expand vocabularies by combining existing morphemes rather than inventing arbitrary forms. Communicative efficiency shapes lexical systems at multiple levels (Gibson et al., 2019), yet morphological composition -- combining morphemes through compounding or affixation -- has rarely been modeled as a historically situated speaker choice among competing morpheme sequences, leaving unanswered why a language settles on one morpheme combination over other plausible alternatives. We ask whether a trade-off between listener recoverability and speaker production cost can predict attested compositions over contemporaneously available alternatives. Here we show, within the Rational Speech Act (RSA) framework (Frank & Goodman, 2012; Goodman & Frank, 2016) using a time-indexed lexicon constructed from Corpus of Historical American English (COHA) and Corpus of Contemporary American English (COCA), that across 4323 naturally occurring English compounds and derivations spanning 1820--2019, attested compositions are systematically ranked above unattested alternatives generated from contemporaneously available morphemes. Models integrating semantic informativeness with production cost outperform semantic-only and cost-only baselines on Mean Reciprocal Rank (MRR) and top-k accuracy (Acc@k), with the advantage of the Pragmatic Speaker model ($S_1$) over the semantic-only baseline growing as the candidate set expands, where meaning alone leaves morphological choice underdetermined. These findings suggest that lexicalization reflects a communicative trade-off between expressiveness and efficiency, extending rational accounts of communication from utterance-level choice to the internal structure of words.

### [76] [Revisiting Graph-Tokenizing Large Language Models: A Systematic Evaluation of Graph Token Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03514)
*Zhongjian Zhang,Yue Yu,Mengmei Zhang,Junping Du,Xiao Wang,Chuan Shi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文挑战了图标记化LLM（GTokenLLM）能够有效理解图token的普遍认知，通过提出统一评估框架GTEval，在格式和内容层面进行指令变换评估，发现现有模型存在过敏感/过不敏感、过度依赖文本推理等问题，且额外指令微调无法完全解决图token理解挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑GTokenLLM是否真正理解图token在自然语言嵌入空间中的语义，而非仅依赖文本上下文进行推理。

Method: 形式化统一GTokenLLM框架，提出GTEval评估流程，通过格式级和内容级指令变换测试模型对图token的理解能力，在6个代表性模型上进行实验。

Result: (1) 现有GTokenLLM未充分理解图token，存在过敏感或过不敏感问题，过度依赖文本推理；(2) 图token虽保留图信息并在各层被关注，但其利用因模型和指令变体而异；(3) 额外指令微调可提升原始/见过指令性能，但无法彻底解决图token理解问题。

Conclusion: GTokenLLM对图token的理解远非充分，现有范式存在根本性局限，需要进一步的改进研究。

Abstract: The remarkable success of large language models (LLMs) has motivated researchers to adapt them as universal predictors for various graph tasks. As a widely recognized paradigm, Graph-Tokenizing LLMs (GTokenLLMs) compress complex graph data into graph tokens and treat them as prefix tokens for querying LLMs, leading many to believe that LLMs can understand graphs more effectively and efficiently. In this paper, we challenge this belief: \textit{Do GTokenLLMs fully understand graph tokens in the natural-language embedding space?} Motivated by this question, we formalize a unified framework for GTokenLLMs and propose an evaluation pipeline, \textbf{GTEval}, to assess graph-token understanding via instruction transformations at the format and content levels. We conduct extensive experiments on 6 representative GTokenLLMs with GTEval. The primary findings are as follows: (1) Existing GTokenLLMs do not fully understand graph tokens. They exhibit over-sensitivity or over-insensitivity to instruction changes, and rely heavily on text for reasoning; (2) Although graph tokens preserve task-relevant graph information and receive attention across LLM layers, their utilization varies across models and instruction variants; (3) Additional instruction tuning can improve performance on the original and seen instructions, but it does not fully address the challenge of graph-token understanding, calling for further improvement.

### [77] [SURE-RAG: Sufficiency and Uncertainty-Aware Evidence Verification for Selective Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03534)
*Jingxi Qiu,Zeyu Han,Cheng Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SURE-RAG提出了一种基于证据充分性验证的选择性RAG回答框架，通过聚合成对声明-证据验证器的局部关系分布，生成可解释的答案级信号（覆盖度、关系强度、不一致性、冲突和检索不确定性），实现支持/反驳/不足三种决策，在HotpotQA-RAG v3基准上达到0.9075 Macro-F1，相比强基线提升显著，同时保持完全可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统将检索等同于验证，但检索到的段落即使与问题相关也可能无法充分证明答案。研究旨在填补这一"证据充分性验证"的空白，建立一种可审计的选择性RAG回答机制。

Method: 提出SURE-RAG框架，基于证据充分性是集合级属性的观察，通过共享的成对级别声明-证据验证器生成局部关系分布，然后聚合为覆盖度、关系强度、不一致性、冲突和检索不确定性等可解释的答案级信号，最终做出三路决策并输出可审计的选择性得分。

Result: 在HotpotQA-RAG v3基准上，校准后的SURE-RAG达到0.9075 Macro-F1，显著高于DeBERTa均值池化（0.6516）和GPT-4o评判（0.7284），与强但不可解释的concat交叉编码器（0.8888）匹配且具备完全可审计性。30%覆盖率下风险从0.2588降至0.1642（减少37%）。在HaluBench不安全检测上SURE-RAG与GPT-4o排名反转（0.3343 vs 0.7389不安全-F1），表明充分性验证与自然幻觉检测是不同问题。

Conclusion: 证据充分性验证与自然幻觉检测是不同的问题任务，SURE-RAG通过可解释的聚合协议在选择性RAG中实现了高效且可审计的证据充分性判断，显著降低了不安全回答的风险。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) grounds answers in retrieved passages, but retrieval is not verification: a passage can be topical and still fail to justify the answer. We frame this gap as evidence sufficiency verification for selective RAG answering: given a question, a candidate answer, and retrieved evidence, predict whether the evidence supports, refutes, or is insufficient, and abstain unless support is established. We present SURE-RAG, a transparent aggregation protocol built on the observation that evidence sufficiency is a set-level property: missing hops and unresolved conflicts cannot be detected by independent passage scoring. A shared pair-level claim-evidence verifier produces local relation distributions, which SURE-RAG aggregates into interpretable answer-level signals -- coverage, relation strength, disagreement, conflict, and retrieval uncertainty -- yielding a three-way decision and an auditable selective score. We evaluate on HotpotQA-RAG v3, a controlled multi-hop benchmark, under an artifact-aware protocol (shortcut baselines, counterfactual swaps, no-oracle checks, GPT-4o audits). Calibrated SURE-RAG reaches 0.9075 Macro-F1 (0.8951 +/- 0.0069), substantially above DeBERTa mean-pooling (0.6516) and a GPT-4o judge (0.7284), while matching a strong but opaque concat cross-encoder (0.8888 +/- 0.0109) with full auditability. Risk at 30% coverage drops from 0.2588 to 0.1642, a 37% reduction in unsafe answers. To deliberately probe the task boundary, we further contrast SURE-RAG with GPT-4o on HaluBench unsafe detection: the ranking reverses (0.3343 vs 0.7389 unsafe-F1), establishing that controlled sufficiency verification and natural hallucination detection are distinct problems.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有专利审查基准将审查视为判别式分类或静态抽取任务，未能捕捉其固有的交互式和迭代式特性（类似于学术出版中的同行评审与 rebuttal 过程）。

Method: 构建 PatRe 基准：包含480个真实专利审查案例，将审查建模为审查意见生成与申请答辩的多轮动态过程，支持oracle（金标准）和检索模拟两种评估设置。

Result: 不同LLM在专利审查任务上表现存在显著差异：专有模型与开源模型之间表现不同，审查方分析与申请方答辩之间也存在任务不对称性。

Abstract: Patent examination is a complex, multi-stage process requiring both technical expertise and legal reasoning, increasingly challenged by rising application volumes. Prior benchmarks predominantly view patent examination as discriminative classification or static extraction, failing to capture its inherently interactive and iterative nature, similar to the peer review and rebuttal process in academic publishing. In this paper, we introduce PatRe, the first benchmark that models the full patent examination lifecycle, including Office Action generation and applicant rebuttal. PatRe comprises 480 real-world cases and supports both oracle and retrieval-simulated evaluation settings. Our benchmark reframes patent examination as a dynamic, multi-turn process of justification and response. Extensive experiments across various LLMs reveal critical insights into model performance, including differences between proprietary and open-source models, as well as task asymmetries between examiner analysis and applicant-side rebuttal. These findings highlight both the potential and current limitations of LLMs in modeling complex, real-world legal reasoning and technical novelty judgment in patent examination. We release our code and dataset to facilitate future research on patent examination modeling.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 闭源模型对提示变化鲁棒性强；领域适配开源模型（MedGemma 3 27B）在合适提示下表现极具竞争力；最终在子任务4（证据引用对齐）获得第1名，子任务3（患者友好答案生成）获得第3名。

Conclusion: 在无训练数据且受隐私约束的低资源临床QA场景中，纯提示工程方法（无需权重更新）是有效的解决方案，开源领域适配模型与恰当提示策略相结合可达到与闭源模型竞争的性能。

Abstract: This paper presents the joint participation of the BIT.UA and AAUBS groups in the ArchEHR-QA 2026 shared task, which focuses on clinical question answering and evidence grounding in a low-resource setting. Due to the absence of training data and the strict data privacy constraints inherent to the healthcare domain (e.g. GDPR), we investigate the capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) without weight updates. We evaluate several state-of-the-art proprietary models and locally deployable open-source alternatives using various prompt engineering strategies, including task decomposition, Chain-of-Thought, and in-context learning. Furthermore, we explore majority voting and LLM-as-a-judge ensembling techniques to maximize predictive robustness. Our results demonstrate that while proprietary models exhibit strong resilience to prompt variations, domain-adapted open-source models (such as MedGemma 3 27B) achieve highly competitive performance when paired with the right prompt. Overall, our prompt-based approach proved highly effective, securing 1st place in Subtask 4 (evidence citation alignment) and 3rd place in Subtask 3 (patient-friendly answer generation). All code, results, and prompts are available on our GitHub repository: https://github.com/bioinformatics-ua/ArchEHR-QA-2026.

### [81] [A Paradigm for Interpreting Metrics and Identifying Critical Errors in Automatic Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03671)
*Thibault Bañeras-Roux,Mickael Rouvier,Jane Wottawa,Richard Dufour*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将选定指标融入最小编辑距离（minED）的新范式，以在保持WER/CER可解释性的同时，更好地反映人工感知的转录错误评估方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WER和CER虽被广泛使用，但与人耳感知相关性差且无法利用语言语义信息；而基于度量的嵌入方法虽然能逼近人工感知，但得分难以解释。因此需要一种兼具可解释性和感知相关性的评估指标。

Method: 提出一种新范式，将选定的感知相关指标融入最小编辑距离（minED）中，从而得到等效于错误率的结果，使转录误差的度量与人工感知对齐。

Result: minED在保持类似WER/CER的可解释性的同时，能够反映错误的人工感知严重程度，并支持从人类视角分析不同错误类型的严重性。

Conclusion: 该范式成功弥补了传统错误率指标与感知嵌入方法之间的鸿沟，提供了一种既可解释又能反映人类感知的ASR评估新方法。

Abstract: The most commonly used metrics for evaluating automatic speech transcriptions, namely Word Error Rate (WER) and Character Error Rate (CER), have been heavily criticized for their poor correlation to human perception and their inability to take into account linguistic and semantic information. While metric-based embeddings, seeking to approximate human perception, have been proposed, their scores remain difficult to interpret, unlike WER and CER. In this article, we overcome this problem by proposing a paradigm that consists in incorporating a chosen metric into it in order to obtain an equivalent of the error rate: a Minimum Edit Distance (minED). This approach parallels transcription errors with their human perception, also allowing an original study of the severity of these errors from a human perspective.

### [82] [A Comprehensive Analysis of Tokenization and Self-Supervised Learning in End-to-End Automatic Speech Recognition applied on French Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03696)
*Thibault Bañeras-Roux,Mickael Rouvier,Jane Wottawa,Richard Dufour*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 需要采用更全面的评估指标来指导ASR系统的超参数和模型选择，以更好适配下游应用需求。

*Zhifeng Hao,Zhongjie Chen,Junhao Lu,Shengyin Yu,Guimin Hu,Keli Zhang,Ruichu Cai,Boyan Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SERE框架，通过基于概念路径度量、句法度量和因果模式过滤的结构化示例检索策略，缓解LLM在事件因果识别中的因果幻觉偏差，提升少样本因果推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在事件因果识别任务中存在因果推理偏差，倾向于过度预测因果关系（即因果幻觉），导致ECI性能受限。

Method: 提出SERE框架，利用三种结构化检索策略：1）概念路径度量（基于ConceptNet编辑距离衡量事件间概念关系）；2）句法度量（基于句法树编辑距离量化结构相似性）；3）因果模式过滤（基于预定义因果结构使用LLM筛选示例）。通过检索更相关的示例指导LLM进行因果推理。

Result: 在多个ECI数据集上的大量实验验证了SERE的有效性。

Abstract: Event Causality Identification (ECI) requires models to determine whether a given pair of events in a context exhibits a causal relationship. While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance across various NLP tasks, their effectiveness in ECI remains limited due to biases in causal reasoning, often leading to overprediction of causal relationships (causal hallucination). To mitigate these issues and enhance LLM performance in ECI, we propose SERE, a structural example retrieval framework that leverages LLMs' few-shot learning capabilities. SERE introduces an innovative retrieval mechanism based on three structural concepts: (i) Conceptual Path Metric, which measures the conceptual relationship between events using edit distance in ConceptNet; (ii) Syntactic Metric, which quantifies structural similarity through tree edit distance on syntactic trees; and (iii) Causal Pattern Filtering, which filters examples based on predefined causal structures using LLMs. By integrating these structural retrieval strategies, SERE selects more relevant examples to guide LLMs in causal reasoning, mitigating bias and improving accuracy in ECI tasks. Extensive experiments on multiple ECI datasets validate the effectiveness of SERE. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/DMIRLAB-Group/SERE.

*Ruichu Cai,Juntao Gan,Miao Mai,Zhifeng Hao,Boyan Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SAM-NER提出基于语义原型中介的三阶段框架，通过领域不变的中间原型空间稳定零样本命名实体识别中的跨域迁移，在CrossNER基准上超越强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零样本NER在大语言模型下面临领域和schema迁移时的语义漂移问题，直接映射实体提及到细粒度目标标签会导致系统性语义偏差。

Method: 三阶段框架：(i) 实体发现——协同提取与共识去噪获取高覆盖高保真实体片段；(ii) 抽象中介——将实体投影到从高层本体抽象中蒸馏得到的通用语义原型空间；(iii) 语义校准——通过约束的、定义对齐的推理，用冻结LLM将原型级预测解析为目标域类型。

Result: 在CrossNER基准上，SAM-NER在跨域设置中持续优于先前强零样本NER基线。

Conclusion: 基于语义原型中介的中间抽象空间能有效缓解领域和schema迁移中的语义漂移，提升零样本NER的跨域泛化能力。

Abstract: Zero-shot Named Entity Recognition (ZS-NER) remains brittle under domain and schema shifts, where unseen label definitions often misalign with a large language model's (LLM's) intrinsic semantic organization. As a result, directly mapping entity mentions to fine-grained target labels can induce systematic semantic drift, especially when target schemas are novel or semantically overlapping. We propose \textbf{SAM-NER}, a three-stage framework based on \emph{Semantic Archetype Mediation} that stabilizes cross-domain transfer through an intermediate, domain-invariant archetype space. SAM-NER: (i) performs \emph{Entity Discovery} via cooperative extraction and consensus-based denoising to obtain high-coverage, high-fidelity entity spans; (ii) conducts \emph{Abstract Mediation} by projecting entities into a compact set of universal semantic archetypes distilled from high-level ontological abstractions; and (iii) applies \emph{Semantic Calibration} to resolve archetype-level predictions into target-domain types through constrained, definition-aligned inference with a frozen LLM. Experiments on the CrossNER benchmark show that SAM-NER consistently outperforms strong prior ZS-NER baselines in cross-domain settings. Our implementation will be open-sourced at https://github.com/DMIRLAB-Group/SAM-NER.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂信息需求涉及并、交、排除等集合组合查询，现有检索范式是否真正满足这些约束还是利用"语义捷径"尚不清楚，需要系统性的可重复性研究来验证。

Method: 在QUEST和QUEST+Variants上对主流检索家族和推理导向方法（如ReasonIR、Search-R1）进行基准测试；引入LIMIT+控制基准，其中相关性依赖于任意属性谓词和约束满足，较少依赖预训练知识。

Result: (i) QUEST上最佳神经检索器Recall@100>0.41，BM25仅0.20，但推理方法不统一优于通用检索器；(ii) LIMIT+上最强QUEST方法从Recall@100≈0.42跌至0.02以下，词汇检索升至~0.96；(iii) 按组合深度分层，所有方法性能持续下降，代数稀疏和词汇方法更稳定，稠密方法崩溃。

Conclusion: 现有神经检索和推理方法在受控组合约束场景下泛化能力不足，词汇方法表现更稳定；发布代码和LIMIT+数据生成脚本以支持未来可重复性研究和受控评估。

Abstract: Complex information needs may involve set-compositional queries using conjunction, disjunction, and exclusion, yet it remains unclear whether current retrieval paradigms genuinely satisfy such constraints or exploit `semantic shortcuts'. We conduct a reproducibility study to benchmark major retrieval families and reasoning-targeted methods on QUEST and QUEST+Variants, and introduce LIMIT+, a controlled benchmark where relevance depends on arbitrary attribute predicates and constraint satisfaction, and less on pretrained knowledge. Our findings show that (i) on QUEST, the best neural retrievers achieve an effectiveness that is more than double what can be achieved with BM25 (Recall@100 ${>}$0.41 vs.\ 0.20), but reasoning-targeted methods like ReasonIR and Search-R1 do not outperform general-purpose retrievers uniformly; (ii) on LIMIT+, gains fail to transfer, where the strongest QUEST method collapses from Recall@100${\approx}$0.42 to below 0.02, while classic lexical retrieval gains to ${\sim}$0.96. Lastly, (iii) stratifying by compositional depth reveals a consistent degradation across all methods, where algebraic sparse and lexical methods show more stable performance while dense approaches collapse. We release code and LIMIT+ data generation scripts to support future reproducibility and controlled evaluation.

Abstract: We introduce TRACE, a cross-domain engineering framework for trustworthy agentic AI in operationally critical domains. TRACE combines a four-layer reference architecture with an explicit classical-ML vs. LLM-validator split (L2a/L2b), a stateful orchestration-and-escalation policy (L3), and bounded human supervision (L4); a metrologically grounded trust-metric suite mapped to GUM/VIM/ISO 17025; and a Model-Parsimony principle quantified by the Computational Parsimony Ratio (CPR). Three instantiations--clinical decision support, industrial multi-domain operations, and a judicial AI assistant--transfer the samearchitecture and metrics across principally different governance contexts. The L2a/L2b separation makes the use of large language models a deliberate design decision rather than an architectural default, with parsimony quantified through CPR. TRACE introduces CPR as a first-class design principle in trustworthy-AI engineering.

We evaluate proprietary and open-source LLM judges using both correctness and inconsistency metrics, distinguishing intrinsic inconsistency under stochastic decoding from procedural inconsistency under prompt and response perturbations. Based on these insights, we introduce Prompt Steering Replacement (PSR) models that estimate token-specific steering coefficients from the activations themselves and are trained to imitate prompt-based interventions. ### [92] [Atomic Fact-Checking Increases Clinician Trust in Large Language Model Recommendations for Oncology Decision Support: A Randomized Controlled Trial](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03916)
*Lisa C. Adams,Linus Marx,Erik Thiele Orberg,Keno Bressem,Sebastian Ziegelmayer,Denise Bernhardt,Markus Graf,Marcus R. Makowski,Stephanie E. Combs,Florian Matthes,Jan C. Peeken*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究原子事实核查（将AI治疗建议分解为可独立验证的声明并链接到源指南文档）相比传统可解释性方法，能否提高临床医生对AI建议的信任度。

Conclusion: 在高风险临床决策中，将AI建议分解为可验证声明并链接源指南的方法，比传统可解释性方法更能显著提升临床医生的信任。

Abstract: Question: Does atomic fact-checking, which decomposes AI treatment recommendations into individually verifiable claims linked to source guideline documents, increase clinician trust compared to traditional explainability approaches?

Traditional transparency mechanisms showed a dose-response gradient of improvement over baseline (d = 0.25 to 0.50).
  Meaning: Decomposing AI recommendations into individually verifiable claims linked to source guidelines produces substantially higher clinician trust than traditional explainability approaches in high-stakes clinical decisions.

### [93] [The Counterexample Game: Iterated Conceptual Analysis and Repair in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03936)
*Daniel Drucker,Kyle Mahowald*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探索语言模型能否通过“定义-反例-修复”的迭代循环进行概念分析。实验发现，LM生成的反例中，LM法官的接受率约是人类的2倍，但两者判断具有一定一致性。迭代过程会使定义变得更冗长而不更准确，且某些概念难以形成稳定定义。总之，LM能参与哲学推理，但迭代收益递减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 概念分析（通过反例不断精炼定义）是哲学方法论的核心。作者希望探究语言模型是否具备这种迭代推理能力，从而检验LM能否从事高层次的哲学推理任务。

Method: 设计迭代分析与修复链：一个LM实例生成反例，另一个LM修复定义，如此循环。对20个概念进行数千次反例-修复循环，并引入人类专家和LM法官对反例有效性进行评判。

Result: 1）LM生成的反例中，LM法官的接受率约为人类专家的2倍；2）人类之间以及人类与LM之间对单个项目的有效性判断具有中等程度的一致性；3）随着迭代次数增加，定义变得更冗长但准确性并未提高；4）某些概念难以形成稳定的定义。

Conclusion: 语言模型能够参与哲学推理中的概念分析，但反例-修复循环的效果会快速递减。该任务可作为评估LM能否进行高水平迭代哲学推理的测试案例。

Abstract: Conceptual analysis -- proposing definitions and refining them through counterexamples -- is central to philosophical methodology. We study whether language models can perform this task through iterated analysis and repair chains: one model instance generates counterexamples to a proposed definition, another repairs the definition, and the process repeats. Across 20 concepts and thousands of counterexample-repair cycles, we find that, although many LM-generated counterexamples are judged invalid by both expert humans and an LM judge, the LM judge accepts roughly twice as many as humans do. Nonetheless, per-item validity judgments are moderately consistent across humans and between humans and the LM. We further find that extended iteration produces increasingly verbose definitions without improving accuracy. We also see that some concepts resist stable definitions in general. These findings suggest that while LMs can engage in philosophical reasoning, the counterexample-repair loop hits diminishing returns quickly and could be a fruitful test case for evaluating whether LMs can sustain high-level iterated philosophical reasoning.

</details>


### [94] [Feature-Augmented Transformers for Robust AI-Text Detection Across Domains and Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03969)
*Mohamed Mady,Johannes Reschke,Björn Schuller*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI生成文本已大规模跨领域、跨生成管线生产，监督式二分类检测器对分布偏移的鲁棒性成为核心需求，现有方法在分布偏移下性能脆弱。

Result: 基座模型在域内达到99.5%平衡准确率；最佳模型DeBERTa-v3-base+FeatAttn在M4上达到85.9%平衡准确率，超过最强零样本基线7.22个百分点；多种子实验证实高稳定性。

Conclusion: 特征增强结合现代DeBERTa骨干显著优于早期BERT/RoBERTa模型；固定阈值协议提供了更真实、更具信息量的实用检测器鲁棒性评估；可读性和词汇特征对分布偏移下的鲁棒性贡献最大。

Abstract: AI-generated text is nowadays produced at scale across domains and heterogeneous generation pipelines, making robustness to distribution shift a central requirement for supervised binary detectors. We train transformer-based detectors on HC3 PLUS and calibrate a single decision threshold by maximising balanced accuracy on held-out validation; this threshold is then kept fixed for all downstream test distributions, revealing domain- and generator-dependent error asymmetries under shift. We evaluate in-domain on HC3 PLUS, under cross-dataset transfer to the multi-domain, multi-generator M4 benchmark, and on the external AI-Text-Detection-Pile. Although base models achieve near-ceiling in-domain performance (up to 99.5% balanced accuracy), performance under shift is brittle and strongly model-dependent. Feature augmentation via attention-based linguistic feature fusion improves transfer, with our best model (DeBERTa-v3-base+FeatAttn) achieving 85.9% balanced accuracy on M4. Multi-seed experiments confirm high stability. Under the same fixed-threshold protocol, our model outperforms strong zero-shot baselines by up to +7.22 points. Category-level ablations further show that readability and vocabulary features contribute most to robustness under shift. Overall, these results demonstrate that feature augmentation and a modern DeBERTa backbone significantly outperform earlier BERT/RoBERTa models, while the fixed-threshold protocol provides a more realistic and informative assessment of practical detector robustness.

### [95] [Logical Consistency as a Bridge: Improving LLM Hallucination Detection via Label Constraint Modeling between Responses and Self-Judgments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03971)
*Hao Mi,Qiang Sheng,Shaofei Wang,Beizhe Hu,Yifan Sun,Zhengjia Wang,Hengqi Zeng,Yang Li,Danding Wang,Juan Cao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出LaaB框架，通过逻辑一致性桥接神经特征与符号判断，利用元判断过程将符号标签映射回特征空间，实现双视角信号的对齐与融合，从而增强大语言模型幻觉检测。在4个数据集、4种LLM、8个基线上的实验证明了其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测方法仅关注单一层面（隐式神经不确定性或显式符号推理），将内在耦合的行为割裂处理，未能利用二者的相互依赖关系以获得整体视角。

Method: LaaB框架通过"元判断"过程将符号标签映射回特征空间，利用响应与元判断标签之间的逻辑一致性（相同或相反）作为桥梁，通过互学习机制对齐和融合神经特征与符号判断的双视角信号。

Result: 在4个公开数据集、4种LLM、8个基线方法的对比实验中，LaaB展现出优越的检测性能。

Conclusion: 神经特征与符号判断的逻辑一致性可作为有效桥梁，双视角融合的互学习策略能够显著提升幻觉检测能力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are prone to factual hallucinations, risking their reliability in real-world applications. Existing hallucination detectors mainly extract micro-level intrinsic patterns for uncertainty quantification or elicit macro-level self-judgments through verbalized prompts. However, these methods address only a single facet of the hallucination, focusing either on implicit neural uncertainty or explicit symbolic reasoning, thereby treating these inherently coupled behaviors in isolation and failing to exploit their interdependence for a holistic view. In this paper, we propose LaaB (Logical Consistency-as-a-Bridge), a framework that bridges neural features and symbolic judgments for hallucination detection. LaaB introduces a "meta-judgment" process to map symbolic labels back into the feature space. By leveraging the inherent logical bridge where response and meta-judgment labels are either the same or opposite based on the self-judgment's semantics, LaaB aligns and integrates dual-view signals via mutual learning and enhances the hallucination detection. Extensive experiments on 4 public datasets, across 4 LLMs, against 8 baselines demonstrate the superiority of LaaB.

</details>


### [96] [EQUITRIAGE: A Fairness Audit of Gender Bias in LLM-Based Emergency Department Triage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03998)
*Richard J. Young,Alice M. Matthews*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EQUITRIAGE对五种LLM在ESI急诊分诊中的公平性审计发现：所有模型性别翻转率均超过5%（9.9%-43.8%），存在不同方向的性别偏差；人口统计学盲化可有效降低部分模型的偏差，但年龄成为残留信息通道；链式思维提示损害所有模型的准确性；组别公平性、反事实不变性和性别校准是三种不同的公平属性，模型间干预效果具有特异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床证据表明急诊分诊中存在持续性性别差异，而医院正在试点LLM作为分诊决策支持工具，亟需评估这些模型是否重现或减轻已知的性别偏见。

Method: 在18,714个MIMIC-IV-ED病例上构建374,275次评估，测试五种LLM（Gemini-3-Flash、Nemotron-3-Super、DeepSeek-V3.1、Mistral-Small-3.2、GPT-4.1-Nano）在四种提示策略下的ESI分配，生成9,346个性别交换的反事实配对，分析翻转率、方向性偏差、校准差异及消融实验。

Result: 所有模型翻转率超5%（9.9%-43.8%）；DeepSeek和Gemini分别表现出女性弱分诊偏差（F/M比2.15:1和1.34:1）；人口统计学盲化将Gemini翻转率降至0.5%，但DeepSeek仍有残留偏差（F/M 1.25）；链式思维提示降低所有模型准确性；消融实验揭示Gemini和DeepSeek相同表型下的不同机制。

Conclusion: 组别公平性、反事实不变性与性别校准是三种不同的公平属性；干预效果具有模型依赖性；在临床部署前应进行逐模型的反事实审计。

Abstract: Emergency department triage assigns patients an acuity score that determines treatment priority, and clinical evidence documents persistent gender disparities in human acuity assessment. As hospitals pilot large language models (LLMs) as triage decision support, a critical question is whether these models reproduce or mitigate known biases. We present EQUITRIAGE, a fairness audit of LLM-based ESI assignment evaluating five models (Gemini-3-Flash, Nemotron-3-Super, DeepSeek-V3.1, Mistral-Small-3.2, GPT-4.1-Nano) across 374,275 evaluations on 18,714 MIMIC-IV-ED vignettes under four prompt strategies. Of 9,368 originals, 9,346 are paired with a gender-swapped counterfactual. All five models produced flip rates above a pre-registered 5% threshold (9.9% to 43.8%). Two showed directional female undertriage (DeepSeek F/M 2.15:1, Gemini 1.34:1); two were near-parity; one had high sensitivity with weak male-direction asymmetry. DeepSeek's directional bias coexisted with a low outcome-linked calibration gap (0.013 against MIMIC-IV admission), a Chouldechova-style dissociation between within-group calibration and between-pair counterfactual invariance. Demographic blinding reduced Gemini's flip rate to 0.5%; an age-preserving blind variant left DeepSeek with residual F/M 1.25, implicating age as a residual channel. Chain-of-thought prompting degraded accuracy for all five models. A two-model ablation reveals opposite underlying mechanisms for the same directional phenotype: in Gemini the signal is emergent in the combined name+gender swap, while in DeepSeek the gender token alone carries it. EQUITRIAGE shows that group parity, counterfactual invariance, and gender calibration are distinct fairness properties, that intervention effectiveness is model-dependent, and that per-model counterfactual auditing should precede clinical deployment.

### [97] [Rethinking Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval: Evaluating and Advancing Retrievers in Agentic Search Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04018)
*Yilun Zhao,Jinbiao Wei,Tingyu Song,Siyue Zhang,Chen Zhao,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出BRIGHT-Pro基准（多方面黄金证据评估）和RTriever-Synth合成语料（方面分解互补正例与硬负例），微调得到RTriever-4B模型，实验表明方面感知和智能体评估能揭示标准指标隐藏的行为，RTriever-4B显著优于基座模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理密集型检索工作在评估和训练上均有限制：基准如BRIGHT仅提供狭窄黄金集并孤立评估检索器，合成训练语料常优化单段落相关性而非证据组合构建。

Method: 构建BRIGHT-Pro专家标注基准（多方面黄金证据），在静态和智能体搜索协议下评估；构建RTriever-Synth方面分解合成语料（互补正例+正例条件硬负例），基于Qwen3-Embedding-4B通过LoRA微调得到RTriever-4B。

Conclusion: 推理密集型检索需要超越单纯主题相似性，构建互补证据组合，方面感知评估和智能体搜索协议能更准确反映检索器在推理场景中的真实表现。

Abstract: Reasoning-intensive retrieval aims to surface evidence that supports downstream reasoning rather than merely matching topical similarity. This capability is increasingly important for agentic search systems, where retrievers must provide complementary evidence across iterative search and synthesis. However, existing work remains limited on both evaluation and training: benchmarks such as BRIGHT provide narrow gold sets and evaluate retrievers in isolation, while synthetic training corpora often optimize single-passage relevance rather than evidence portfolio construction. We introduce BRIGHT-Pro, an expert-annotated benchmark that expands each query with multi-aspect gold evidence and evaluates retrievers under both static and agentic search protocols. We further construct RTriever-Synth, an aspect-decomposed synthetic corpus that generates complementary positives and positive-conditioned hard negatives, and use it to LoRA fine-tune RTriever-4B from Qwen3-Embedding-4B. Experiments across lexical, general-purpose, and reasoning-intensive retrievers show that aspect-aware and agentic evaluation expose behaviors hidden by standard metrics, while RTriever-4B substantially improves over its base model.

### [98] [Safety and accuracy follow different scaling laws in clinical large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04039)
*Sebastian Wind,Tri-Thien Nguyen,Jeta Sopa,Mahshad Lotfinia,Sebastian Bickelhaup,Michael Uder,Harald Köstler,Gerhard Wellein,Sven Nebelung,Daniel Truhn,Andreas Maier,Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出SaFE-Scale框架，系统评估临床大语言模型安全性与模型规模、证据质量、检索策略、上下文长度和推理计算的关系。基于RadSaFE-200基准测试（200道放射学多选题），评估34个模型在六种部署条件下的表现。研究发现干净证据可显著提升安全指标（准确率从73.5%提升至94.1%，高风险错误降至2.6%），而标准RAG、Agentic RAG、最大上下文提示和额外推理计算均无法复现该安全效益。结论：临床LLM安全并非规模扩展的被动结果，而是由证据质量、检索设计、上下文构建和集体失败行为共同决定的部署属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有临床大语言模型研究通常通过扩大模型规模、增加上下文长度、提升检索复杂度或增加推理计算来提升性能，隐含假设是更高准确性意味着更安全的行为。但在医学领域，少数自信的、高风险的、或与证据矛盾的错误可能比平均基准性能更为关键，因此需要系统性地评估安全性在不同部署条件下的变化。

Method: 提出SaFE-Scale框架，引入RadSaFE-200基准（放射学安全评估200题，含医生定义的干净证据、冲突证据和选项级标签）。在六种部署条件下评估34个本地部署的LLM：闭卷问答（零样本）、干净证据、冲突证据、标准RAG、Agentic RAG、最大上下文提示。评估指标包括准确率、高风险错误率、证据矛盾率和危险过度自信率。

Result: 干净证据带来最强的安全改进：准确率从73.5%提升至94.1%，高风险错误从12.0%降至2.6%，矛盾率从12.7%降至2.3%，危险过度自信从8.0%降至1.6%。标准RAG和Agentic RAG未能复现该安全轮廓；Agentic RAG虽提升了准确率和降低了矛盾率，但高风险错误和危险过度自信仍较高。最大上下文提示增加了延迟但未缩小安全差距；额外推理计算仅带来有限收益。最坏情况分析显示，临床严重后果的错误集中在一小部分问题上。

Conclusion: 临床LLM的安全性并非模型规模扩展的被动副产物，而是一个由证据质量、检索设计、上下文构建和集体失败行为共同塑造的部署属性。单纯依赖扩展模型或增加计算资源无法系统性地保障临床安全。

Abstract: Clinical LLMs are often scaled by increasing model size, context length, retrieval complexity, or inference-time compute, with the implicit expectation that higher accuracy implies safer behavior. This assumption is incomplete in medicine, where a few confident, high-risk, or evidence-contradicting errors can matter more than average benchmark performance. We introduce SaFE-Scale, a framework for measuring how clinical LLM safety changes across model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute. To instantiate this framework, we introduce RadSaFE-200, a Radiology Safety-Focused Evaluation benchmark of 200 multiple-choice questions with clinician-defined clean evidence, conflict evidence, and option-level labels for high-risk error, unsafe answer, and evidence contradiction. We evaluated 34 locally deployed LLMs across six deployment conditions: closed-book prompting (zero-shot), clean evidence, conflict evidence, standard RAG, agentic RAG, and max-context prompting. Clean evidence produced the strongest improvement, increasing mean accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1%, while reducing high-risk error from 12.0% to 2.6%, contradiction from 12.7% to 2.3%, and dangerous overconfidence from 8.0% to 1.6%. Standard RAG and agentic RAG did not reproduce this safety profile: agentic RAG improved accuracy over standard RAG and reduced contradiction, but high-risk error and dangerous overconfidence remained elevated. Max-context prompting increased latency without closing the safety gap, and additional inference-time compute produced only limited gains. Worst-case analysis showed that clinically consequential errors concentrated in a small subset of questions. Clinical LLM safety is therefore not a passive consequence of scaling, but a deployment property shaped by evidence quality, retrieval design, context construction, and collective failure behavior.

</details>

# cs.GT [[Back]](#toc)

### [99] [Fast Strategy Solving for the Informed Player in Two-Player Zero-Sum Linear-Quadratic Differential Games with One-Sided Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03112)
*Mukesh Ghimire,Zhe Xu,Yi Ren*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文针对有限时域两人零和微分博弈中一类具有单边收益信息的不完全信息博弈问题，提出了一种高效的子博弈求解算法。通过将P1的纳什均衡计算转化为双层优化问题（外层优化信号策略，内层为博弈树LQR），并采用伴随反向传播求解，在8维状态空间、2维动作空间中实现了约10Hz的实时求解，为信息不对称下的鲁棒博弈规划提供了可行方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究揭示了非线性动力学和收益下G的NE原子结构，但将近似方案实现为实时子博弈求解尚未达成，而实际应用中存在仿真到现实的差距且需要鲁棒控制，亟需高效的在线求解方法。

Method: 将P1的NE计算转化为双层优化问题：外层优化"信号"策略（何时及如何通过控制揭示信息），内层为博弈树LQR求解最优闭环控制。采用伴随反向传播方案：先进行"反向"LQR传递，再进行"正向"梯度下降传递以改进信号策略。

Result: 在8维状态空间、2维动作空间、离散时间步K=10的归航问题变体上，算法实现了约10Hz的子博弈求解频率，能够在信息不对称和随机扰动下进行鲁棒的博弈论规划。

Conclusion: 本文提出的双层优化与伴随反向传播方法显著提升了不完全信息微分博弈中子博弈求解的计算效率，为信息不对称场景下的实时鲁棒控制提供了有效的理论基础和算法实现。

Abstract: We study finite-horizon two-player zero-sum differential games with one-sided payoff information ($G$), where the informed player (P1) knows the game payoff, while P2 only has a public belief over a finite set of possible payoffs. In this case, P1's Nash equilibrium (NE) behavioral strategy may control the release of the type information or even resort to manipulate P2's belief. Previous studies revealed an atomic structure of the NE of $G$ with general nonlinear dynamics and payoffs, leading to tractable NE approximation. Implementing such approximation schemes for real-time sub-game solving, however, has not been achieved, yet is desired for applications where sim-to-real gaps exist and robust control is required. This paper improves the computational efficiency of sub-game solving for P1 during $G$ with linear dynamics and quadratic losses. Specifically, we show that P1's NE computation can be formulated as a bi-level optimization problem where the outer level optimizes the "signaling" strategy, i.e., when and how to reveal information through control, and the inner level is a game-tree LQR that solves for the optimal closed-loop control. This bi-level problem is solved via an adjoint-enabled backpropagation scheme: A "backward" LQR pass is followed by a "forward" gradient descent pass for improving the signaling. We apply the proposed algorithm to approximate NEs for variants of a homing problem with a 8D state space, 2D action spaces, and a discrete time horizon of $K=10$. The algorithm achieves $\approx$10Hz sub-game solving, enabling robust game-theoretic planning under information asymmetry and random disturbances.

</details>


### [100] [Unsecured Lending via Delegated Underwriting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03307)
*Diego Estevez*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需抵押、法律身份或中心化承销的匿名用户无担保借贷机制。新借款人通过担保人委托信用额度进入系统，违约损失沿担保链回溯，还款则创造" earned credit"以扩展未来借贷能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在去中心化或匿名环境中，传统的无担保借贷依赖法律身份、抵押品或中心化信用评估，但这些在伪匿名用户群体中不可行。现有方案要么要求超额抵押（如DeFi借贷），要么依赖链下身份系统，限制了资本效率或去中心化程度。本文旨在设计一种纯链上、无抵押、基于社交担保的信用借贷机制。

Method: 设计了一种委托机制：新借款人必须由现有用户（担保人）委托部分信用额度才能进入系统，担保人的信用容量会相应减少。系统维护" earned credit"（通过还款积累）和" delegated credit"（委托额度）。违约损失沿担保路径回溯，由担保人承担；还款则增加借款人的 earned credit，提升其未来借贷能力。通过设置 earned credit 增长上限来防止"先还款再违约"的套利行为。

Result: 证明了委托机制能够保持总信用容量守恒（不会凭空创造新额度）；撤销和违约的影响仅局限在唯一担保路径上；简单的 earned credit 增长上限能够使"先还款再违约"策略弱无利可图（weakly unprofitable）。

Conclusion: 该机制为无抵押链上借贷提供了一种可行的去中心化信用分配方案，通过社交担保和信用回溯机制在不依赖外部身份或抵押品的情况下实现风险隔离和激励相容。

Abstract: We develop a mechanism for unsecured lending among pseudonymous users that does not rely on collateral, legal identity, or centralized underwriting. New borrowers enter only through sponsors who delegate part of their own credit capacity, so onboarding a new account reallocates existing borrowing power rather than minting new capacity. Default losses flow back along the sponsor path, while repayment creates earned credit that expands future borrowing capacity. We prove that delegation conserves aggregate credit capacity, that revocation and default remain local to a unique sponsor path, and that a simple cap on earned-credit growth makes repay-then-default weakly unprofitable.

</details>

### [104] [Skew polycyclic over finite chain rings associated to trinomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03164)
*Maryam Bajalan,Edgar Martínez-Moro,Hassan Ou-azzou*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究有限链环上由中心三项式定义的斜多循环码，在非交换（斜）背景下考察其汉明等价性。通过引入三项式上的等价关系（基于带有Schur乘法的二项式群的群论刻画），证明了斜多循环码与由特定三项式 $x^n-(x^\ell+1)$ 定义的码在汉明等价意义下可归约到规范情形，并利用底层链环的单位群分解确定了相应等价类的大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为有限链环上由中心三项式定义的斜多循环码建立系统的汉明等价分类理论，将复杂的分类问题简化为规范形式，从而降低此类码的构造与分析难度。

Method: 在非交换（斜）环上定义三项式的等价关系，利用Schur乘法给出该等价关系的群论刻画；证明斜多循环码的汉明等价性可归约到规范三项式 $x^n-(x^\ell+1)$；通过底层链环的单位群分解计算等价类的大小。

Result: 建立了三项式等价关系与群论刻画之间的联系，证明了任意斜多循环码汉明等价于由规范三项式定义的码，并给出了等价类大小的精确计算公式。

Conclusion: 该工作为有限链环上斜多循环码的汉明等价分类提供了一种完整的理论框架，将问题归结为规范情形，并得到了等价类的计数结果，有助于进一步理解非交换编码理论中的结构性质。

Abstract: This work studies skew polycyclic codes over finite chain rings defined by central trinomials. For this class of codes, we investigate Hamming equivalence in the non-commutative (skew) setting. We introduce an equivalence relation on the defining trinomials and demonstrate that it admits a group-theoretic characterization in terms of a group of binomials equipped with the Schur multiplication. We determine the conditions under which skew polycyclic codes are Hamming equivalent to those defined by the specific trinomial $x^n-(x^\ell+1)$. This reduces the classification problem for these codes, up to Hamming equivalence, to a canonical case. Finally, we determine the size of the corresponding equivalence class using the decomposition of the unit group of the underlying chain ring.

### [105] [Single-Period Portfolio Selection via Information Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03184)
*Bo-Yu Yang,Michael Gastpar*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文通过信息论视角研究CRRA效用下的单期投资组合选择问题，证明了CE增长率可分解为Rényi散度、Rényi熵和对配分函数项，并展示了CRRA组合选择等价于Rényi信息投影问题，提出了一种Blahut-Arimoto式交替优化算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将CRRA效用下的投资组合选择问题纳入信息论框架，揭示风险厌恶系数与Rényi阶数之间的操作意义对应关系，并开发更高效的优化算法。

Method: 利用Rényi散度和熵的信息论工具，对有限支撑市场收益向量下的CRRA效用组合选择进行精确分解；通过Rényi信息投影的变分表示，推导出具有闭式辅助更新和KL型组合步的Blahut-Arimoto式交替优化算法。

Result: CRRA效用下的CE增长率可分解为Rényi散度、Rényi熵和对配分函数三项；风险厌恶系数恰好等于Rényi阶数；提出的交替优化算法在低风险厌恶区域比直接CRRA优化和Cover方法需要更少的迭代次数。

Conclusion: CRRA投资组合选择与Rényi信息投影等价，所提算法在低风险厌恶区域具有效率优势。

Abstract: We study the single-period portfolio selection problem under Constant Relative Risk-Aversion (CRRA) utility through the information-theoretic lens. Assuming only that the market payoff vector has finite support, we show that the Certainty-Equivalent (CE) growth rate under CRRA utility can be exactly decomposed into a portfolio-induced Rényi divergence term, a Rényi entropy term of the risk-tilted market law, and a log-partition term. In this setting, the Rényi order has a clear operational meaning: it exactly coincides with the investor's coefficient of relative risk aversion. We further show that CRRA portfolio selection is equivalent to a Rényi information-projection problem. Using a variational representation of Rényi divergence, we obtain a Blahut-Arimoto-style alternating optimization with a closed-form auxiliary update and a KL-type portfolio step. In the low risk-aversion regime, this method empirically requires fewer iterations than both direct CRRA utility optimization and Cover's method.

### [106] [Generalized Function-Correcting Partition Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03370)
*Charul Rajput,Mahak,V. Lalitha*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出广义函数纠错分区码（GFCPC），统一了函数纠错分区码和带数据保护的函数纠错码，通过多步构造和距离需求矩阵表征最优冗余，证明该框架比现有方案具有更低的冗余。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有函数纠错分区码（FCPC）仅能保护多个函数具有相同纠错级别，而带数据保护的函数纠错码仅能为数据和一个函数分配不同保护级别。实际场景中需要同时保护多个分区（每个分区对应不同函数或数据），且各分区可能要求不同的最小汉明距离（不同纠错强度）。现有方案无法灵活应对这种多层级、多分区的差异化保护需求。

Method: 提出GFCPC框架，定义距离需求矩阵D来形式化每个分区的距离要求；给出多步构造过程（通过实例演示）；推导最优冗余的通用上界（考虑分区组合的联合）和下界；对二元域上的两个分区，在特定邻域条件下建立改进的下界；用距离需求矩阵D将最优冗余刻画为关联D-码的最短长度问题。

Result: 理论推导了GFCPC的冗余上界和下界；通过多个示例证明，GFCPC的冗余可以严格小于以下两种方案：1）各分区独立FCPC冗余之和；2）为联合分区设计单个最高距离FCPC的冗余。表明GFCPC在差异化保护中具有更优的冗余效率。

Conclusion: GFCPC统一并推广了FCPC和带数据保护的函数纠错码，为多分区差异化错误保护提供了更紧凑的冗余框架。距离需求矩阵D为最优冗余的分析提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We introduce generalized function-correcting partition codes (GFCPCs) that simultaneously protect multiple partitions of the message space against different numbers of errors. Given partitions with respective distance requirements, a GFCPC is a systematic encoding that guarantees, for each partition, a specified minimum Hamming distance between codewords whose messages lie in different blocks. This framework unifies and generalizes both function-correcting partition codes, which protect multiple functions with a common error-correction level, and function-correcting codes with data protection, which assign different levels of protection to data and a single function. We present a multi-step construction procedure for these codes and demonstrate it with some examples. We derive general upper and lower bounds on the optimal redundancy, including the upper bound which considers the join of different combinations of the partitions. We define the distance requirement matrix $\mathcal{D}$ for the GFCPCs and use it to characterize the optimal redundancy in terms of the shortest length of an associated $\mathcal{D}$-code. For two partitions of message space over the binary field, we establish improved lower bounds on the optimal redundancy under specific neighborhood conditions on the partitions. Through several examples, we demonstrate that the proposed framework can yield strictly smaller redundancy than both the sum of the individual FCPC redundancies and the redundancy of a single FCPC designed for the join partition with the highest distance (strongest protection required).

</details>


### [107] [Pareto-type finite-block optimality for source codes: a constrained Markov example](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03552)
*Stefano Della Fiore*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究约束马尔可夫源下可逆源编码的有限块帕累托最优性。通过Dalai-Leonardi的四符号约束马尔可夫源实例，构造了一种基于信息代价排序的规范单射二元映射，证明了该编码的平均块长严格小于3n/2，且与最优编码存在Ω(1/√n)的差距，表明该编码不是帕累托最优的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究约束源编码中有限块长度下的帕累托最优性概念，以Dalai-Leonardi提出的"有意义的例子"作为可完全分析的具体测试案例，检验其编码是否在有限块平均长度意义下达到帕累托最优。

Method: 通过信息代价K(u)排序（先按K(u)递增，再按长度和字典序）构造规范单射二元映射C，将允许字符串映射到短字典序二元串。利用信息代价对允许字符串进行精确枚举，并利用短字典序间隙恒等式证明每个代价类在长度K(u)-1和K(u)之间均匀分割。

Result: 证明了𝔼[|C(X₁)|]=3/2，对n≥2有𝔼[|C(X₁ⁿ)|]<3n/2，且对任意0<c<√2/(18√π)，对所有足够大n有𝔼[|C(X₁ⁿ)|]≤3n/2-c/√n，即与3n/2存在Ω(1/√n)的差距。

Conclusion: 该可逆Dalai-Leonardi编码在有限块平均长度意义下不是帕累托最优的，表明即使在这个简单示例中，约束源编码的有限块帕累托比较也能揭示编码性能的实质性差异。

Abstract: We study a Pareto-type notion of finite-block optimality for injective source codes, where two codes are compared through the full sequence of expected block lengths. As a concrete and fully analyzable test case, we revisit the four-symbol constrained Markov source introduced by Dalai and Leonardi in their "meaningful example'' on constrained-source decodability. For each admissible nonempty string $u=x_1^m \in \mathscr{A} \subset \mathscr{X}^+$, let $$ K(u):=-\log_2 \mathbb{P}(X_1^m=u) $$ denote its information cost. We construct a canonical injective binary mapping $C:\mathscr{A} \to \{0,1\}^+$ by ordering admissible strings by increasing $K(u)$, then by length and lexicographic order, and assigning binary strings in shortlex order. For the length-$n$ block $X_1^n$ we prove $$ \mathbb{E}[|C(X_1)|]=\tfrac32, \qquad \mathbb{E}[|C(X_1^n)|]<\tfrac32\,n\quad (n\ge 2). $$ Moreover, for every fixed $$ 0<c<\frac{\sqrt2}{18\sqrtπ} $$ we have $$ \mathbb{E}[|C(X_1^n)|]\le \tfrac32\,n-\frac{c}{\sqrt n} $$ for all sufficiently large $n$. Thus, for this source, the reversible Dalai-Leonardi code is not Pareto-optimal with respect to finite-block average length. The proof is based on an exact enumeration of admissible strings by information cost and on a shortlex gap identity implying that each cost class splits evenly between lengths $K(u)-1$ and $K(u)$. The example is simple, but it already exhibits the kind of finite-block Pareto comparison that seems natural for injective source coding under source constraints.

</details>


### [108] [New bounds on the covering radius of orthogonal arrays of even strength](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03589)
*Peter Boyvalenkov,Ferruh Ozbudak,Maya Stoyanova*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对二元强度为2k的正交阵列的覆盖半径，提出了新的线性规划（LP）构造性下界和改进的LP上界方法，并通过对BCH、Melas和Zetterberg码对偶族的研究，利用代数曲线技术获得了紧致的覆盖半径估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有覆盖半径界（如Tietäväinen界或Fazekas-Levenshtein界）在非紧致正交阵列（即基数严格超过Rao下界）时不够优，需要更精确的界来刻画覆盖半径。

Method: 1. 提出两种LP上界方案：当覆盖半径最远点不与y对径时，得到优于Tietäväinen界的上界；当所有最远点的对径点在C中时，得到依赖于基数C的上界。2. 利用代数曲线技术对BCH、Melas、Zetterberg码对偶族推导下界。

Result: 获得了三个无穷族二元正交阵列的覆盖半径的上下界，两者在某些情形下非常接近。

Conclusion: 新的LP方法在非紧致情形下优于经典界，结合代数曲线技术可得到更精确的覆盖半径估计。

Abstract: We obtain new linear programming (LP) and constructive bounds for the covering radius of binary orthogonal arrays of strength $2k$. Our LP bounds develop in two alternative scenarios. First, if a point $y \in F_2^n$, where the covering radius of some orthogonal array $C \subset F_2^n$ of strength $2k$ is realized, is such that the farthest point of $C$ to $y$ is not antipodal to $y$ we obtain a bound which is better than the Tiet{ä}v{ä}inen (or Fazekas-Levenshtein) bound for non-tight arrays (i.e., the cardinality strictly exceeds the Rao lower bound). Second, if all points where the covering radius is realized are such that their antipodes are in $C$, we obtain a bound which depends on the cardinality of $C$ and is again better whenever the orthogonal array is not tight. We further describe three infinite families of binary orthogonal arrays related to the duals of BCH, Melas, and Zetterberg codes. For these families, we derive lower bounds on the covering radius by applying techniques from algebraic curves over finite fields, while the improved linear programming methods developed in this paper provide upper bounds, leading in some cases to fairly close estimates.

</details>

As a result, for the short high-rate codes considered, we obtain models that closely approach MLD performance using small datasets and proper training. Our findings also suggest that many prior results for SBND models in the literature underestimate their true correction capability due to undertraining. Code to reproduce all results is available at: https://github.com/lebidan/sbnd.

Abstract: Building scalable quantum computers requires quantum error-correcting codes that enable reliable operations in the presence of noise. CE systematically derives analytic expressions for the Bhattacharyya parameters of the bit-channels of a given discrete BMS channel at arbitrary polarization levels. CE also enables structural analysis, providing new evidence of extremality of the binary erasure channel (BEC) and binary symmetric channel (BSC) through the lens of complex analysis, and revealing new channel-dependent recursions for a class of BSC bit-channels.

### [112] [Joint Design of Piggyback and Conjugate Transformation Functions for Repair Bandwidth Reduction in Piggybacking Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03991)
*Hao Shi,Zhengyi Jiang,Gefeng Deng,Zhongyi Huang,Hanxu Hou*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出共轭捎带码（conjugate-piggybacking codes），通过联合设计捎带函数与共轭变换，在高码率分布式存储系统中实现更优的节点修复带宽，在中等域大小上保持MDS性质，相比现有方案降低了修复带宽和期望修复流量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有捎带码（piggybacking codes）在保持MDS性质时对捎带函数设计有严格限制，导致修复带宽降低效果有限。本文旨在突破这一限制，在小子分组化下进一步提升高码率纠删码的修复效率。

Method: 提出共轭捎带码，核心创新在于联合设计捎带函数与共轭变换（conjugate transformations），在中等域大小（$\mathbb{F}_{2^8}$）上保持MDS性质的同时优化修复带宽。具体包括：使部分校验节点达到最优修复带宽，整体修复带宽优于现有捎带码方案。

Result: 在$\mathbb{F}_{2^8}$高码率设置下，共轭捎带码的修复带宽持续低于现有捎带码，且期望修复流量优于传统RS码修复。代价是域大小略有增加，体现了修复效率与域开销之间的实际权衡。

Conclusion: 共轭捎带码在高码率分布式存储场景下提供了更优的修复效率，以轻微域大小开销换取显著的修复带宽降低，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Efficient node repair is a central requirement in distributed storage systems, particularly in high-rate erasure-coded deployments where repair traffic directly affects network overhead and recovery cost. Piggybacking codes reduce the repair bandwidth of MDS array codes while keeping the sub-packetization level small. However, existing piggybacking constructions often rely on restrictive piggyback-function designs to preserve the MDS property over small fields, which limits their repair-bandwidth reduction. We propose {\em conjugate-piggybacking} codes, a new class of MDS array codes that jointly design piggyback functions and conjugate transformations under small sub-packetization. The proposed construction improves repair efficiency while preserving the MDS property over moderate field sizes. In particular, it enables some parity nodes to achieve optimal repair bandwidth and reduces the overall repair bandwidth compared with existing piggybacking-based designs. We analyze the MDS property and repair bandwidth of the proposed codes and evaluate them against existing piggybacking codes under high-code-rate settings over $\mathbb{F}_{2^8}$. We further conduct a repair-traffic simulation under uniform single-node failures to quantify the expected traffic reduction in storage-oriented settings. The results show that our construction consistently achieves lower repair bandwidth than related piggybacking codes and reduces expected repair traffic compared with conventional RS repair. These gains are obtained at the cost of a slightly larger field size, revealing a practical trade-off between repair efficiency and field-size overhead for high-rate distributed storage.
